<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
      
      document.addEventListener('click', (evt) => {
        if ( evt.target.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'input' && evt.target.id === 'checkTerms' ) {
          let closestButton = [...evt.target.closest('form').elements].filter(elem => elem.getAttribute('type') === 'submit')[0]

          if ( evt.target.checked ) {
            $(closestButton).removeClass('disabled')
            $(closestButton).prop('disabled', false)
          } else {
            $(closestButton).addClass('disabled')
            $(closestButton).prop('disabled', true)
          }
        }
      })
      

      const checkerIIFE = (() => {

        let assignElements = setInterval(() => {
            if ( document.getElementById('checkTerms') && document.getElementById('checkboxMozillaMini') && navigator.userAgent ) {
              	let isFirefox = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('firefox') > -1;
              	console.log('assigned');
              	keepGoing( isFirefox )
                clearInterval( assignElements )
            } else {
              	console.log('assigning')  
            }
        }, 200)
	
		function keepGoing( isFirefox ){
          
          if ( isFirefox ) {
            console.log('Using firefox');
            let showIt = setInterval(() => {
            	if ( document.getElementById('checkboxMozillaMini').style.display == 'block' ) {
                } else {
					document.getElementById('checkboxMozillaMini').style.display = 'block';
                }
				
			}, 150)
            
            document.addEventListener('click', (evt) => {
              if ( evt.target.id === 'checkboxMozillaMini' ) {
              	document.getElementById('checkTerms').click()

                if ( document.getElementById('checkTerms').checked ) {
                  document.getElementById('checkboxMozillaMini').style.background = '#807c7c'
                } else {
                  document.getElementById('checkboxMozillaMini').style.background = ''
                }
                
              }
            })
          } else {
            console.log('Using any other browser, not firefox');
          }
      }

      })()
    
    });

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

<script>
var features_home = function(){
    var init = function(){
        scripts();
    }

    var scripts = function(){
        console.log("Run Recommended home");
		var categories = []
        var x = document.querySelectorAll(".productRecommended");
      	console.log(x);
      
      	var i;
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
          var collectionData = x[i].getAttribute('section-data')
          var classCollection = "collectionType_" + collectionData

          
          let elem = document.querySelector ('.productRecommended')
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName('collectionsFilters')[0] ){
          	elem.innerHTML = elem.innerHTML + '<div class="container containerFeatures"><header class="section__header"><div class="section__header-stack"><h2 class="section__title heading h3">Productos recomendados</h2></div><div class="collectionsFilters"></div></header></div>';
          }
          
          let elemFilter = document.querySelector ('.collectionsFilters')
          var active = '';
          var vitrineClass = 'vitrine_' + classCollection;
          x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add(vitrineClass)
          if( i == 0 ){
          	active = 'active'
            x[i].getElementsByClassName('containerSectionFeatures')[0].classList.add('active')
          }
          if( !document.getElementsByClassName(classCollection)[0] ){
          	elemFilter.innerHTML = elemFilter.innerHTML + '<div class="itemCollection '+classCollection+' '+active+'" namefilter="'+classCollection+'">'+collectionData+'</div>';
          }
        }
      
      
      	setTimeout(function(){
          const box = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Gatos ');
		  box.click()
          const box2 = document.querySelector('.collectionType_Perros ');
		  box2.click()
        }, 500);
      
      
      
        // Listen for all clicks on the document
        document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!event.target.closest('.itemCollection')) return;
            // Otherwise, run our code...
          	console.log(event);
          	var classBtn = event.path[0].getAttribute('namefilter')
            var classVitrine = 'vitrine_' + classBtn;
           
          
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".itemCollection");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("active");
            });
          	var elems = document.querySelectorAll(".containerSectionFeatures");
            [].forEach.call(elems, function(el) {
                el.classList.add("nodispaly");
            });
          
          	console.log(classVitrine);
          
          	document.getElementsByClassName(classBtn)[0].classList.add('active')
            document.getElementsByClassName(classVitrine)[0].classList.remove('nodispaly')
         
        }, false);
      
      

    } // 
    return {
        init: init,
        scripts: scripts
        
    }
}();
features_home.init();
</script>

  <div class="container"><div class="html rte">
      <h1 class="h1home">Supermercado Agropecuario Tierragro</h1>
    </div>
  </div>
</section>

</div><div id="shopify-section-1631828111ef9d71c5" class="shopify-section"><section class="section" data-section-id="1631828111ef9d71c5" data-section-type="image-with-text">
  <div class="container"><div class="image-with-text"><div class="image-with-text__image-container" style="width: 50%;"><div class="aspect-ratio" style="padding-bottom: 66.66666666666667%"><img class="lazyload image--fade-in" data-src="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0410/2199/7206/files/tierragro-supermercado-agropecuario-home_{width}x.jpg?v=1631831117" data-widths="[300,400,500,600]" data-sizes="auto" alt="supermercado agropecuario">

            <noscript>
              <img src="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0410/2199/7206/files/tierragro-supermercado-agropecuario-home_800x.jpg?v=1631831117" alt="supermercado agropecuario">
            </noscript>
          </div></div>
        <div class="image-with-text__text-container">
        <div class="image-with-text__text-aligner"><div class="rte">
            <p>Somos un <strong>supermercado agropecuario</strong> con más de 25 años de trayectoria. En nuestras tiendas puedes encontrar desde una puntilla hasta un tractor. </p><p>Nuestro equipo está capacitado en diferentes profesiones como <strong>veterinarios, agrónomos, ingenieros mecánicos</strong> y personal experto en cada área. Contamos con un amplio catálogo de productos para: <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/perros" title="Perros">perros</a>, <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/gatos" title="Gatos">gatos</a>, <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/equinos" title="Equinos">equinos</a>, <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/otas-especies-aves" title="Aves">aves</a> y otras especies, como también <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/maquinaria" title="Maquinaria">maquinaria</a>, <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/agro" title="Agro">equipos para el agro</a> y el <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/jardineria" title="Jardín">jardín</a>. </p><p>Facilitamos la adquisición de <strong>productos para el campo</strong>, brindando logística, soporte y financiación para el agricultor. Ofrecemos servicios de <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/pages/peluqueria-para-mascotas" title="Peluquería para mascotas">peluquería para mascotas</a> y <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/pages/centro-veterinario" title="Centro Veterinario">centro veterinario</a>. También juguetes, alimentación para mascotas y accesorios. En nuestro supermercado agropecuario contamos con una oferta de más de 10.000 productos en diferentes categorías como <strong>nutrición para mascotas</strong>,<strong> </strong>farmacia, vacunas, productos de aseo y cosméticos, marroquinería, accesorios para mascotas y equinos, maquinaría, <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/equipos-de-fumigacion-agro" title="Equipos de Fumigación ">equipos de fumigación</a>, elementos de protección personal, ferretería, herramientas, semillas, jardinería, <a href="https://www.tierragro.com/collections/fertilizantes-agro" title="Abonos">abonos</a>, fertilizantes, entre otros productos de nutrición vegetal y protección de cultivos como también algunos productos comestibles.</p>
<a href="/collections/all" class="button button--primary">Ver Productos</a></div>

        <script data-cfasync="false">
          jQuery(function(){
            jQuery(document).on('click', "input[name='checkout']:not(.saso-ignore), input[value='Checkout']:not(.saso-ignore), button[name='checkout']:not(.saso-ignore), [href$='checkout']:not(.saso-ignore), button[value='Checkout']:not(.saso-ignore), input[name='goto_pp'], button[name='goto_pp'], input[name='goto_gc'], button[name='goto_gc']", function(e){
              e.preventDefault();

              if (typeof sasoCheckout != "function") {
              	window.location = "/checkout";
              }

              jQuery.ajax({
                          cache: false,
                          contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                          dataType: "json",
                          type: "GET",
                          url: '/cart.js',
                          success: function(res) {
                            window.saso.cart = res
                            sasoCheckout()
                          }
                        })

            });
          });
        </script>
